To Validate The Comments For The Post Made By Specific User

To validate if length of body in the comment is not less than given characters

Scenario Outline

Given userId is obtained by searching username "<userName>"
And list all the posts written by the user using userId
When list all the comments for the posts made by user
Then validate that the length of text body in the comment is not less than "<commentLength>" characters

Examples: 

# User Name Comment Length
1 Bret 40
2 Delphine 30
Steps Outcome
Example: {userName=Bret, commentLength=40}
SUCCESS 20.23s
Given userId is obtained by searching username "Bret"
SUCCESS 9.9s
GET https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users?username=Bret

Response

Status code: 200

Content Type: null
